<date>1575170773382<//date><rating>5< /rating>< Text>
This is my absolute favorite Boba place. I've been to other Boba places around Ventura and Santa Barbara and they are quite honestly very bougie and just not as good as Bigstraw Boba. Bigstraw is just amazing. You can easily see the passion for what they do, and it comes out in just how delicious the drinks are. They're simple, but that's how it should be. Easy to understand ingredients with a lot of modifications to reduce the sugar, or replace ingredients if you have allergies. The number of flavors they have is mind-blowing - there truly is something for everyone and you can't go wrong. Also, as an artist I have to say 8 love their aesthetic and that logo design is great.

I tell literally everyone I know that Bigstraw Boba is the absolute best.< /Text>

< review>
My car is falling apart... And then I got hit in an accident.  I was not looking forward to having my car in the shop, as my last experience at a body shop was absolutely  dreadful. So, I pop into the shop... first, I noticed that the lobby is full of retro appliances etc etc and the coffee table is a repurposed engine... I SO need one of those!
So, I fill out forms, and Derrick is the man assigned to work with me (poor guy)
They get me to my rental place and I get the word it will be about a week.
My ride was ready in LESS than that time, and was fixed better than what it looked like before it was hit.
Derrick was honest with me, and didn't make promises he couldn't keep. He let me know if they found something wrong and they did great work.
About an hour after I picked up my ride... as my luck would have it. I blew a radiator hose. Unbelievably, Derrick offered to have it fixed, with me paying for the hose. It was not even related to the body issue, and the crew at South Bay was gonna take care of it.
Now, I was able to fix it... But the fact that they would take care of me when not even necessary, is priceless. They set themselves apart from any other body shop.
They also gave me candy, which my daughter loved.
If and when I crash again, they will be the ONLY place I get my car fixed at.
I ALSO reccommended them to Enterprise for thier corporate accounts. . . Because that's what you do when you appreciate great work<//review>

111675655856518218213<//userid>
<name>Christine Yabuda<//name><Date>1569515218168< /Date><rating>5</rating>< review>
Welcome to Torrance, Scoops! They just did a soft opening starting today!!! Go there cause it's delicious for all ice cream lovers including non-dairy people. I was so excited to eat that I didn't even take a pic of my ice cream! Rookie mistake.

A small little shop in the Nijiya plaza with ample parking, unfortunately not a ton of seating inside. Some bench seating against the wall, but a ton of flavors including 8 regular ice cream flavors and 4 non-dairy flavors made with oat milk! Prices are reasonable and the scoops portions are huge. I went for the one scoop with two flavors, which is really 2 scoops, and it was basically a meal in itself. They also will use your own bowl if you present them with it. Sampling is allowed and the guy there was super nice and friendly.

MAPLE NON VEGAN CHOCOLATE CHIP (NON-DAIRY)
This doesn't taste like oat milk at all! I love that it's creamy and not icy like other non-dairy ice creams can be. A very subtle maple flavor with tiny chocolate chips. So simple, yet so delicious.

ALMOND CARDAMON BURNT SUGAR (NON-DAIRY)
Loved this one. As a gluten free person, I miss out on textures in food. The burnt sugar really added a crumb like texture that really made me keep eating spoonful after spoonful of this one. The almond and cardamon are perfect accents to make this ice cream nicely complex.< /review>

5<//rate>
< text>
Such a good value for great tasting ice cream and unique flavors! Must come!

I kept thinking they were undercharging me, how could 2 huge scoops of ice cream be just $3?? They consider "One Scoop" to be 2 huge scoops. and a "Kids Scoop" to be 1 scoop. WOW!

The staff is super nice and helpful with trying flavors. After trying many interesting flavors which rotate out each day, I settled on this winning combo:

**Peanut butter curry ice cream + vanilla Jim beam cheesecake was an amazing combo**

However if you just go in and try a bunch of flavors and don't get anything, there is a $1 tasting fee for all you freeloaders! C'mon it's only $3- I haven't seen anything like this steal in a long while!

The neighborhood this is in is very cool. The businesses on this intersection of Heliotrope and Melrose have good vibes and are trendy. Lots of restoration - renovated apartments, gastropubs, ice cream, clothing stores. It's off the beaten path of the more popular part of Melrose, but definitely worth the visit!</text>

< Text>
Terra has not supported their products.  We purchased over $50,000 of individual stainless fan filter units from them.  Most if not all of them have FAILED independent HEPA testing.  Leaks in the housing, leaks around the filter seal, etc.  Bad engineering design with no mechanical way to ensure filter seal.

Plain and simple, these do not meet the ISO or Grade classification their website claims.  Then good luck getting them to do anything else except send you some silicone caulk and say good luck.  Our production has been shut down because of these issues for months.  We have called and emailed multiple times.  Customer service doesn't seem to think this is urgent enough to answer the phone or call back within 24 hrs...

As you can see in the picture below.  Terra sent out multiple filters without doing particulate testing to verify integrity.  The only testing they do is differential testing, not filter integrity testing. You can see in the picture below when we analyzed the filter media further, there were tears in the media.  They did not offer to replace the almost 10 filters we found issues with....  We have been forced to trash the filters and start from scratch with another manufacturer.

Bottom line is low quality and bad customer service is what we have experienced.   They don't stand behind their products.</Text>
